<t>CREATE TABLE courses (
    course_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    course_name VARCHAR(255),
    instructor_name VARCHAR(255),
    credits INT
);

CREATE TABLE students (
    student_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    student_name VARCHAR(255),
    email VARCHAR(255),
    course_id INT REFERENCES courses(course_id)
);

CREATE TABLE assignments (
    assignment_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    assignment_name VARCHAR(255),
    course_id INT REFERENCES courses(course_id),
    due_date DATE
);

CREATE TABLE submissions (
    submission_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    student_id INT REFERENCES students(student_id),
    assignment_id INT REFERENCES assignments(assignment_id),
    submission_date DATE,
    grade FLOAT
);</t><s>UPSERT INTO courses (course_id, course_name, instructor_name, credits) VALUES (1, 'Mathematics', 'Prof. Smith', 3) ON CONFLICT (course_id) DO UPDATE SET course_name = excluded.course_name, instructor_name = excluded.instructor_name, credits = excluded.credits;</s>

<t>CREATE TABLE courses (
    course_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    course_name VARCHAR(255),
    instructor_name VARCHAR(255),
    credits INT
);

CREATE TABLE assignments (
    assignment_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    assignment_name VARCHAR(255),
    course_id INT REFERENCES courses(course_id),
    due_date DATE
);

CREATE TABLE students (
    student_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    student_name VARCHAR(255),
    email VARCHAR(255),
    course_id INT REFERENCES courses(course_id)
);

CREATE TABLE submissions (
    submission_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    student_id INT REFERENCES students(student_id),
    assignment_id INT REFERENCES assignments(assignment_id),
    submission_date DATE,
    grade FLOAT
);</t><s>UPSERT INTO courses (course_id, course_name, instructor_name, credits) VALUES (1, 'Mathematics', 'Prof. Smith', 3) ON CONFLICT (course_id) DO UPDATE SET course_name = excluded.course_name, instructor_name = excluded.instructor_name, credits = excluded.credits;</s>
